    SELECT TOP(1) [g].[Id], [g].[CreatedDate], [g].[Description], [g].[Name], [g].[Price], [g].[StockCount]
    FROM [Games] AS [g]
    WHERE [g].[Id] = @__id_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [g0].[Id], [g0].[CategoryId], [g0].[GameId], [c].[Id] AS [Id0], [c].[Name]
    FROM [GameCategories] AS [g0]
    INNER JOIN [Categories] AS [c] ON [g0].[CategoryId] = [c].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[GameId]
LEFT JOIN [GameImages] AS [g1] ON [t].[Id] = [g1].[GameId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [g2].[Id], [g2].[DiscountId], [g2].[GameId], [d].[Id] AS [Id0], [d].[Value]
    FROM [GameDiscounts] AS [g2]
    INNER JOIN [Discounts] AS [d] ON [g2].[DiscountId] = [d].[Id]
) AS [t1] ON [t].[Id] = [t1].[GameId]
ORDER BY [t].[Id], [t0].[Id], [t0].[Id0], [g1].[Id], [t1].[Id]

FROM (
    SELECT TOP(1) [g].[Id], [g].[CreatedDate], [g].[Description], [g].[Name], [g].[Price], [g].[StockCount]
    FROM [Games] AS [g]
    WHERE [g].[Id] = @__id_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [g0].[Id], [g0].[CategoryId], [g0].[GameId], [c].[Id] AS [Id0], [c].[Name]
    FROM [GameCategories] AS [g0]
    INNER JOIN [Categories] AS [c] ON [g0].[CategoryId] = [c].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[GameId]
LEFT JOIN [GameImages] AS [g1] ON [t].[Id] = [g1].[GameId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [g2].[Id], [g2].[DiscountId], [g2].[GameId], [d].[Id] AS [Id0], [d].[Value]
    FROM [GameDiscounts] AS [g2]
    INNER JOIN [Discounts] AS [d] ON [g2].[DiscountId] = [d].[Id]
) AS [t1] ON [t].[Id] = [t1].[GameId]
ORDER BY [t].[Id], [t0].[Id], [t0].[Id0], [g1].[Id], [t1].[Id]
